Sad Presidents Collection Released

WASHINGTON, July 15, 2022 - The official DUSA NFT collection has been released: https://grandbazar.io/collection/dusa-one-trillion-dollar-coins

‚ÄúShould President Obama be willing to print a $1 trillion platinum coin if Republicans try to force America into default? Yes, absolutely,‚Äù said Paul Krugman, the famous American economist.

To attract more attention to our initiative, we decided to mint one trillion debt dollars NFT coins (OTDC) that we will distribute for free among the most active community members.

The total number of all OTDCs will equal the level of the US National Debt and consist of several editions released gradually after reaching important initiative milestones.

The first edition is named ‚ÄúSad Presidents,‚Äù which includes five coins nominated for $1tn each.

It symbolizes the feelings of famous American leaders of the past, who have devoted their lives to the prosperity of the US and happened to travel through time to modern days.
